[3844] "What does that have to do with F?" Yuria asked.
[3845] "In hexadecimal, the number on the ones place goes up to 15…" Fujisawa said. "But we only have the numbers 0 to 9 in the decimal system. If we only use the numbers 0 to 9, hexadecimal cannot be used. So… in general, the numbers 10 to 15 are represented by the letters A, B, C, D, E, F. F is the 15 in the decimal system. Just like the 9 in the decimal system, F is the largest single digit in hexadecimal."
